        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">"Kaidou of the Beasts"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百獣のカイドウ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hyakujū no Kaidō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, English versions: "Kaido, King of the Beasts")</span><sup id="cite_ref-Epithet_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Epithet-10">[10]</a></sup><br>"The Strongest Creature"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">最強の生物</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Saikyō no Seibutsu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span><sup id="cite_ref-Strongest_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Strongest-11">[11]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup><br>"Wise King"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">明王</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Myōō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, English versions: "Deity")</span><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-wise_king_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wise_king-12">[12]</a></sup></div>
</div>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Fish-Fish Fruit, Model: Azure Dragon<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup><br>Fish-Fish Fruit, Azure Dragon Model<sup id="cite_ref-sbs98_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs98-17">[17]</a></sup></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Fish, Azure Dragon</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible" style="color: #000000;">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: #1C77A7">Devil Fruit</th></tr>

<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Fish-Fish Fruit, Model: Azure Dragon<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup><br>Fish-Fish Fruit, Azure Dragon Model<sup id="cite_ref-sbs98_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs98-17">[17]</a></sup></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Fish, Azure Dragon</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_922" title="Chapter 922">Chapter 922</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Kaidou of the Beasts</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-mag14_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mag14-18">[18]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bounty_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-14">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Epithet_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Epithet-10">[10]</a></sup> renowned as the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a>'s <b>"Strongest Creature"</b>,<sup id="cite_ref-c697p2_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c697p2-19">[19]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Strongest_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Strongest-11">[11]</a></sup> is the <a href="/wiki/Admiral_(Fleet_Captain)" title="Admiral (Fleet Captain)">Governor-General</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a><sup id="cite_ref-c922p10_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922p10-6">[6]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bounty_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-14">[14]</a></sup> and was formerly one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> that ruled over the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Four_Emperors_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Four_Emperors-5">[5]</a></sup> He is also the father of <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c977_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c977-20">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c979_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c979-21">[21]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-daughter_Yamato_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-daughter_Yamato-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p><p>Once a promising child soldier at the service of the <a href="/wiki/Vodka_Kingdom" title="Vodka Kingdom">Vodka Kingdom</a> decades ago, Kaidou was drafted against his will by the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> but managed to escape and start a career in <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">piracy</a>. He was invited by <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a> to join the legendary <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> as an <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Apprentice" title="Pirate Apprentice">apprentice</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c957_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957-4">[4]</a></sup> where he met and befriended <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a> when the Rocks Pirates met their downfall, Linlin provided Kaidou with the rare <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a>. He then went on to form his own crew and build it up into a powerful military force determined to challenge the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>.
</p><p>After being invited to <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> by <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Higurashi" title="Kurozumi Higurashi">Kurozumi Higurashi</a>, Kaidou joined forces with Wano Country's <a href="/wiki/Shogun" title="Shogun">shogun</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Wano_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wano-23">[23]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> and occupied <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> as his base.<sup id="cite_ref-c920p17_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920p17-9">[9]</a></sup> After a failed attempt by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> to overthrow him, he continued to accrue military might in Wano for 20 years before deciding to dispose of Orochi and proceed with his plan for the <a href="/wiki/New_Onigashima_Project" title="New Onigashima Project">New Onigashima Project</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup> Forming a <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Alliance" title="Pirate Alliance">Pirate Alliance</a> with Big Mom, Kaidou intended to seize the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapons</a> and claim the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup> The plan never came to fruition, however, as <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Onigashima was raided</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> on that very same night and the Beasts Pirates were ultimately defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-c1049_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1049-26">[26]</a></sup> Following Kaidou's defeat at <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>'s hands, the <a href="/wiki/World_Economy_News_Paper" title="World Economy News Paper">World Economy News Paper</a> released a new listing of the Four Emperors, with Kaidou no longer being included among them anymore.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> After his defeat, Kaidou is now referred to in Wano's folklore retelling as <b>"Dragon King Kaidou"</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">龍王カイドウ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ryūō Kaidō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou was first referred to by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc" title="Post-Enies Lobby Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</a> when he revealed the existence of the Four Emperors,<sup id="cite_ref-Four_Emperors_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Four_Emperors-5">[5]</a></sup> and was then first directly mentioned by <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-First_Mention_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-First_Mention-29">[29]</a></sup> with his status as one of the Four Emperors revealed after the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> defeated Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup> Thus, Kaidou is the third Emperor mentioned by name and the last to debut.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup> Before he debuted in person, his voice was heard in a flashback that <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a> had when first disembarking on <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c701_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c701-31">[31]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his actions, he can be considered the overarching antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa_Saga" title="Dressrosa Saga">Dressrosa Saga</a>, the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Saga" title="Wano Country Saga">Saga</a>, and a major antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/The_Final_Sea:_The_New_World_Saga" title="The Final Sea: The New World Saga">second half</a> of the series.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8194" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of Kaidou's title as the world's 'Strongest Creature'?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Kaidou's title as the 'Strongest Creature' signifies his unmatched power and dominance in the world of One Piece. This title is not just for show, as Kaidou has demonstrated his immense strength on numerous occasions. He can send people flying with a single swing of his kanabo, broke past Luffy's Gear 4 with great ease, and once sunk nine enormous prison ships singlehandedly. His strength earned him the respect of his vicious companions even as a mere apprentice in the Rocks Pirates. His bounty of 4,611,100,000 is the third-highest known bounty of any pirate, further emphasizing his formidable reputation.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8195" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How did Kaidou transition from being a child soldier to a feared pirate?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Kaidou's journey from a child soldier to a feared pirate is a tale of resilience and ambition. He was frequently caught and escaped from the Marines, earning him a starting bounty of 70,000,000. At the age of fifteen, he became renowned in Hachinosu and was soon recruited by the notorious Rocks Pirates. However, the Rocks Pirates were defeated by Garp and Roger when Kaidou was just twenty-one. Undeterred, he continued his pirate career and at thirty-one, he was approached by Kurozumi Higurashi to assist Orochi in taking over Wano. Kaidou's reputation grew as he demonstrated his power and ruthlessness, even attempting to break the spirits of captured pirates to turn them into soldiers for his crew.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8196" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">Who invited Kaidou to join the legendary Rocks Pirates and why?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Edward Newgate, also known as Whitebeard, invited Kaidou to join the infamous Rocks Pirates. This decision was influenced by Kaidou's impressive strength and combat skills, which he demonstrated on the Pirate Island Hachinosu. Kaidou's addition to the crew made waves in the pirate world, further enhancing the reputation of the Rocks Pirates. Kaidou's strength and dominance within the group made him a key member of the crew.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8197" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is known about Kaidou's relationship with his child, Yamato?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Kaidou's relationship with his son, Yamato, is quite strained and tumultuous. Yamato idolizes Kaidou's enemy, Kozuki Oden, which has led to significant conflict between them. When Yamato expressed a desire to be like Oden, Kaidou reacted by keeping Yamato imprisoned on Onigashima from the age of eight. This harsh treatment has led Yamato to sever ties with Kaidou and openly defy his control over Wano.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8198" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How did Kaidou manage to escape from the Marines?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Kaidou's escapes from the Marines were quite the spectacle. Initially, Kaidou's home country of Vodka Kingdom traded him to the Marines in exchange for the right to participate in the Levely. Kaidou escaped from the ship, which earned him his starting bounty of 70,000,000. Later, he would allow himself to be captured, enjoy the food on the battleships, and then escape with relative ease. His strength and resilience played a significant role in his escapes. He's survived multiple execution attempts because every execution weapon would break when used on him. At one point, he was held captive within the Marine research institute on Punk Hazard, during which time Vegapunk obtained his Lineage Factor. 
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kaidou is a middle-aged man who cuts an imposing figure due to his extreme height of 710 cm<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup> and the bulk of his muscles, making him dwarf normal humans. Overly top-heavy in build, he has a well-muscled torso with wide-set shoulders, thick arms,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup> and somewhat out-of-proportion legs; far less heavily built than his arms yet about the same length (with his feet much tinier than his hands).<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c924_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924-34">[34]</a></sup> Kaidou's head, atop his bulky neck, is disproportionally small as well (smaller than his hands) and has a massive pair of gray-white, sharp-pointed horns coming out of its sides, curving slightly to the front, then upward. During his final fight with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, Kaidou's left horn is broken off.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> He has a longish face with a heavy, hairless brow ridge<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup> topping sharp, often bloodshot eyes (parent to small, yellow irises),<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> plus, a hook nose and a large, full-lipped mouth. Kaidou is near-always seen frowning and is moderately wrinkled: particularly prominent being his crow's feet below his eyes, forehead lines, and laugh lines from always sneering. His black hair consists of an unruly, mostly swept-back mane down to his mid-back, which forms distinctly flat, rectangular locks of which some fall down near the front, over his ears, or jut upward. His facial hair is done in a wavy, waist-length <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fu_Manchu_mustache" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fu Manchu mustache">Fu Manchu mustache</a> that pairs with a spiked goatee across his chin.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p><p>Right of Kaidou's defined abs is his only scar: a massive, recessed X-shape whose upper points reach to his pectoral,<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup> given to him by <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c970_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970-37">[37]</a></sup> Twenty years later, <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> managed to add another scar to Kaidou's chest that runs from the top left point of the first scar to near his left shoulder.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> A tattoo of dull-red segments resembling reptilian scales, individually bordered in orange, goes from Kaidou's left pectoral down the front of his left arm, ending in correspondence to the wrist with a white (dark in the manga), traditionally shaped skull on the lower forearm.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p><p>Clothing-wise, Kaidou dons a blue purple, feathered, sleeveless overcoat draped on his shoulders, and below a lavender, tight-fitting, open shirt with long sleeves.<sup id="cite_ref-c824p10_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824p10-39">[39]</a></sup> He has a black bracelet with golden (dark in the manga) spikes above each wrist. Upholding said shirt is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Makuuchi#Yokozuna" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Makuuchi">thick, off-white belt of laid rope</a> festooned with a pair of white, hanging <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shide_(Shinto)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shide (Shinto)">shide</a> in the front. More outwardly from below the rope hang two additional pieces of fabric: rectangular, hemmed flaps (which may be the bottom of said shirt) that each have, from two hemmed holes at their bottom, a short, thick, golden torus chain attached to themselves. Two yellow straw cords are below the shimenawa, serving as waistbands to secure a short, hanging row of thin, red ribbons. Finally, the rest of his lower wear consists of simple, baggy pants of gray-green color, tucked below the knees into simple, black boots.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup> After his battle against the Big Mom, Kaidou is seen wearing a white version of his usual shirt, which exposed the middle of his body.
</p><p>20 years before the current storyline, Kaidou's Fu Manchu was only chest-length, he lacked his current beard, had much fewer wrinkles, and until his battle with Oden did not have any visible scars on him.<sup id="cite_ref-c920p8_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920p8-40">[40]</a></sup> While he was already very large and muscular back then, he was better proportioned compared to his current top-heavy build. When he was facing Gecko Moria, Kaidou wore a green-blue, open vest and black pants with a thick metal belt. During Oden's execution, he wore the pairing of a dark-blue, sleeveless leather jacket and dark-blue, tight leather pants, with a belt featuring his crew's <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a> on its big, round, gold-framed buckle, in red color on a dark background, alongside black shoes. Additionally, he already wore his purple coat and spiked bracelets. At the time he was seen, due to the injury he suffered from fighting Oden, Kaidou's chest and abdomen were heavily bandaged up.<sup id="cite_ref-c971_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c971-41">[41]</a></sup>
</p><p>As a ten-year old child, Kaidou had shorter shoulder-length hair and wore a scarf. By the time he was 13, he wore a belt across his torso.
</p>
