</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/SBS105_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230624080649" class="image"><img alt="SBS105 Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="66" data-image-name="SBS105 Kaidou.png" data-image-key="SBS105_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7e/SBS105_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20230624080649" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Oda's depiction of Kaidou's face when he eats umeboshi.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kaidou is a merciless, aggressive, and confident warrior who never misses an opportunity to gain an advantage in war.<sup id="cite_ref-VsShanks_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VsShanks-42">[42]</a></sup> He suffers from bouts of apathy and boredom, harboring a general sense of unconcern for most things including the very nature of the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a> and the lives of himself and his subordinates. He keeps a grumpy disposition with little pleasure and excitement in his life and is constantly frowning most of the time. As such, he craves excitement and chaos, wanting to start the largest war in the world because he felt it was too mundane.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> This was true even during his childhood as a soldier under the service of the <a href="/wiki/Vodka_Kingdom" title="Vodka Kingdom">Vodka Kingdom</a>, with a young Kaidou barely showing interest in anything outside of constant warfare.<sup id="cite_ref-child_Kaidou_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-child_Kaidou-44">[44]</a></sup>
</p><p>Apparently, Kaidou always had issues with the world he lived in, particularly the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>, whose authority he did not respect due to his beliefs that the true worth of someone could only be gauged in the battlefield.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> In the past, Kaidou once believed that only he could change the world, supposedly in an attempt to mimic <a href="/wiki/Joy_Boy" title="Joy Boy">Joy Boy</a> and his legend; however, Kaidou has admitted that his methods and overall goal ended up being far different.<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_King_meet_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_King_meet-46">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_King_and_Joy_Boy_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_King_and_Joy_Boy-47">[47]</a></sup> Still, Kaidou remains curious about Joy Boy and whether anyone else is capable of taking up their mantle.<sup id="cite_ref-c1014_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1014-48">[48]</a></sup> He also thinks that Joy Boy could be the one person capable of ever taking him down.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">It may not be the way of the times anymore... but death is what truly completes a person!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kaidou to the Nine Red Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c994_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c994-49">[49]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
Kaidou's recklessness, coupled with his apparent inability to die from any execution method, has caused him to make attempted suicide as his hobby.<sup id="cite_ref-hobby_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hobby-50">[50]</a></sup> Kaidou overall has a very positive view on death, thinking that it is the moment a person achieves true glory. As such, he admires those who die fighting until the very end, such as <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, and acknowledges the impact they end up causing in those moments.<sup id="cite_ref-c994_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c994-49">[49]</a></sup> Kaidou is quite excited and has genuine respect and admiration for any enemy who is actually capable of facing him in combat; however, due to his desire for death, he is quite disappointed when they are unable to defeat him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1013_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1013-51">[51]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Kaidou_Drunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20170226234158" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Drunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou Drunk.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Drunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Kaidou_Drunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170226234158"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Kaidou_Drunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20170226234158" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Drunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Kaidou_Drunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170226234158" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou Drunk.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Drunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Kaidou_Drunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170226234158"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_Drunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A drunken Kaidou drowns his sorrows.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou is a heavy drunkard who loves to drink sake to drown his sorrows, which causes his mood to change erratically when he becomes inebriated. For example, he quickly went from being melancholic over his inability to increase the number of his Gifters and fulfill his dream of having a crew consisting of only Devil Fruit users to becoming angry and violent, brutally beating his subordinates and cursing <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> While drunk, Kaidou may become more destructive by accident since he ends up caring little for his surroundings, to the detriment of his own crew and their operations. In fact, Kaidou is such a habitual drinker that he even dislikes being sober at any given time.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> His drunken mood swings have been exploited in battle as well through a special fighting style known as <a href="/wiki/Shuron_Hakke" title="Shuron Hakke">Shuron Hakke</a>, which, by Kaidou's own admission, is only used on opponents that give him a challenge.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou is greatly annoyed at the number of people capable of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, stating that the world does not need so many people who could use it.
</p><p>Like several other characters, Kaidou has a unique <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">laughing style</a>: "Worororo"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ウォロロロ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Worororo</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-c824p13_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824p13-55">[55]</a></sup> When he is drunk, it sometimes changes to "Fuhihihi"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">フヒヒヒ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Fuhihihi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-c922p8_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922p8-56">[56]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Warmongering">Warmongering</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">We're going to take all of those pampered noble-born rulers and drag them off their ivory thrones down to the battlefield with us! That's what I call <b>equality and freedom</b>! A world where <b>war</b> decides a man's true worth!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kaidou rallying his forces.<sup id="cite_ref-Speech_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Speech-57">[57]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
As far back as his childhood in Vodka, Kaidou was already very familiar with war and seemingly desired for nothing more than endless combat. This upbringing seemingly influenced his values to revolve around war prowess and, as such, he views the battlefield as a sacred place, and any disturbances to a fight as unjust for taking away a battle's freedom. This is a major factor in his ambition to start a giant war: bringing his form of equality and freedom to the world governed by the World Nobles.<sup id="cite_ref-child_Kaidou_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-child_Kaidou-44">[44]</a></sup> Interestingly, despite his declarations opposing the government and its higher ups, Kaidou also provides his supposed enemies with several weapons of his own making (using <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a> and <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> as intermediaries), further showing that he cares more about the war itself than whoever wins it.
</p><p>With the goal of waging an all-out "final war" against the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, Kaidou ultimately seeks to form the strongest pirate crew consisting only of Devil Fruit users, so he actively seeks out formidable manpower in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> to recruit into his growing army, including <a href="/wiki/Super_Rookie" title="Super Rookie">Super Rookies</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> like <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a>, and <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a>. Rather than kill those who resist him, he attempts to break their spirit through torture and forced labor until they either die or submit to his cause.<sup id="cite_ref-Hawkins_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hawkins-58">[58]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> Kaidou also has an interest in finding the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapons</a> and the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> for his cause, having taken a Road Poneglyph under his ownership and ruthlessly hunted down <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, as well as his three retainers, <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin'emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</a>, in the chance that Oden may have imparted some knowledge to them.<sup id="cite_ref-c818_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c818-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou's lust for power led him to invest greatly into various scientific means to create armies, ignoring any side effects and failures. He dreamed of creating a crew completely composed of Devil Fruit users, thus he mass purchased <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILEs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Devil_Fruit" title="Artificial Devil Fruit">Artificial Devil Fruits</a> with a 90% rate of forcing the eaters to laugh but not gain any powers, to feed to many of his subordinates. Kaidou also purchased the Government's failed attempts of creating <a href="/wiki/Gigantification" title="Gigantification">artificial Ancient Giants</a>, all of whom are of low intelligence, to form his combat subdivision, the <a href="/wiki/Numbers" title="Numbers">Numbers</a>. Although these actions greatly bolstered his crew's might, it also led to many of them suffering, such as the "Pleasures" subdivision losing their ability to express any emotions other than laughter while being unable to swim, or the difficult to control Numbers to cause much collateral damage when fighting.
</p><p>Despite his love for battle, Kaidou is pragmatic enough to avoid conflict that could potentially devastate his forces and territories. When <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> attempted to invade Wano Country, Kaidou feared it would become an all-out war and furiously ordered his crew to stop her, especially after being aware that Big Mom's powerful children were accompanying her. This was true even in the past, when Oden returned to Wano Country from his journey. Kaidou agreed with Orochi to trick Oden into submission by making a fake deal with him, giving himself time to reinforce his army. Kaidou even admitted to being unsure of fighting Oden during the time of their first meeting, acknowledging the <a href="/wiki/Daimyo" title="Daimyo">daimyo</a>'s infamous bold nature.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Savagery_and_Barbarism">Savagery and Barbarism</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Friendship is a sham! It's all for show! Deep down, they fear you! You must rule with strength! You are the child of ogres! You are not meant to be friends with humans!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kaidou to his offspring, <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 190px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Oni_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20240420020349" class="image"><img alt="Oni Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="190" height="271" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Oni Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Oni_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Oni_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20240420020349"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Oni_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20240420020349" class="image"><img alt="Oni Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Oni_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20240420020349" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="190" height="271" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Oni Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Oni_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/70/Oni_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20240420020349"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oni_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou's monstrous demeanor.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Akin to the reputation of an oni, Kaidou is savage and brutal and believes that might makes right, using his near unrivaled power to govern others through fear and intimidation while making examples of them should they ever decide to not obey or rebel against his rule. Kaidou, interestingly, does not seem to view himself as a human at all, fiercely thinking that his lineage should not hold a friendly relationship with other humans, but rather distrust and oppose them, under the reasoning that the latter are unable to view the former as anything else than monsters. This is likely due to his experiences as a child, as he grew up as a soldier fighting for the Vodka Kingdom at a young age, only to be betrayed and sold off by his own country because they feared him.
</p><p>Kaidou is extremely cruel, even towards children. After murdering Oden, he viciously insulted the man right in front of his son Momonosuke, adding mockery to the boy's sorrow and hopelessness.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup> Adding to this, he brutally attacked <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Kurozumi Tama</a> and practically left her for dead.<sup id="cite_ref-c923p6_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c923p6-62">[62]</a></sup> Kaidou also bluntly informed <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a> about <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a>'s "death" while casually laughing at Queen's despair over the death of his idol and later found amusement upon seeing Orochi's spiteful execution of Yasuie as well as his ally's cruelty in feeding his own citizens faulty <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE fruits</a>. As an abusive father, Kaidou had no qualms beating up his son Yamato since childhood, showing that even his own child is not spared from his violence and brutality.
</p><p>Kaidou is known to be hard to reason with and not usually open for negotiations or excuses, making it unwise to provoke or underestimate him; this is enforced dramatically when <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, a former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> and former World Noble known for his fearless attitude, became disturbed at the prospect of angering Kaidou when he became potentially unable to fulfill his end of their business deal.<sup id="cite_ref-Joker's_worry_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Joker's_worry-63">[63]</a></sup> One of his crewmates later stated that Kaidou would be very angry once he heard the news of the <a href="/wiki/SMILE_Factory" title="SMILE Factory">SMILE Factory</a>'s destruction, leading to a squad of them attempting to loudly deliver the information from a distance in order to avoid any potential retaliation.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> Despite this, Kaidou is not completely impossible to reason with, demonstrated by his capacity to form an alliance with another Emperor he had attempted to kill days prior.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arrogance_and_Respect_for_Power">Arrogance and Respect for Power</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kaidou venerates strength and military might above all else, with those ideas being the foundation behind his constant amassing of strong subordinates and numerous weapons. He follows the philosophy of "survival of the fittest" and that most problems can be resolved through brute force, agreeing with <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Higurashi" title="Kurozumi Higurashi">Kurozumi Higurashi</a> about that being the way human history has always functioned. Those set of beliefs also appear to be the reason that Kaidou despises the World Nobles and their massive power and influence, which are primarily based on birthright alone instead of any actual combat merit.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Kaidou is highly confident in his power and considers himself to be far above the likes of Super Rookies from the Worst Generation, to the point of even refusing to take the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a> seriously despite them crippling his SMILE trade; this is reinforced by his belief that defeating a Warlord of the Sea is nothing to be impressed with and subsequent dismissal of Doflamingo as being weak.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> He was quick to threaten to kill Big Mom when she announced her intention to come to his territory, showing no reservations against someone possessing power equivalent to his own.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-66">[66]</a></sup> Kaidou seemingly enjoys taking direct attacks from enemies he perceives as strong in order to test their strength, doing so with much amusement.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup> He gladly received attacks from Luffy, Law, Kid, Zoro and Killer, and showed real excitement when they had actually managed to cause him harm, which only made him even more motivated about fighting them.
</p><p>Despite his immense arrogance, Kaidou does acknowledge other individuals of exceptional strength, such as Ashura Doji and Eustass Kid, wishing to have both become subordinates of his despite their constantly defiant attitude. This extends to Luffy, one of the people responsible for the halting of his SMILE trade that was vital to Kaidou's ultimate goals, yet the Emperor chose to have the Straw Hat captain imprisoned so he could be recruited as a soldier of formidable power instead of killing him. Due to his respect for power, Kaidou is willing to offer strong subordinates a chance to be promoted to an All-Star in his crew as long as they prove it in an authorized challenge against a current one. Since Kaidou sees and acknowledges an enemy's power, he does not blame his subordinates for losing battles against opponents that he deems appropriately powerful. Kaidou forgave <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> for losing to <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> in their <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> forms, because he understands that Jack is not weak, but rather that his enemies were merely too strong to handle.<sup id="cite_ref-c991_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c991-68">[68]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Honor_and_Treachery">Honor and Treachery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">I'm sorry about that <b>idiot</b> earlier... I didn't want to win that way.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kaidou apologizing to Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c1044_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1044-69">[69]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
While Kaidou is vicious and ruthless to his enemies, he also showcases a form of strong personal honor and pride to how he fights. When he met Big Mom again for the first time in decades, he told his men to take her Seastone cuffs off before trying to kill her personally in a duel, strictly preferring to fight his enemy fair and square despite having an easier chance to kill his fellow Emperor in a weakened state.
</p><p>Another example of Kaidou's code is that he utterly despises any interference in struggles between himself and an opponent he deems worthy of fighting, and will absolutely not forgive anyone who does so as far killing them as punishment. When a member of the Beasts Pirates seemingly captured Momonosuke (in truth Higurashi in <a href="/wiki/Mane_Mane_no_Mi" title="Mane Mane no Mi">disguise</a>) as a hostage to distract Oden, Kaidou only took the opportunity to strike Oden down because he did not know of the situation until afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-c970p14_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970p14-70">[70]</a></sup> Intolerant of foul play in regard to his own battles, Kaidou killed Higurashi for interfering regardless of her being one of Orochi's closest supporters, and upon witnessing the <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">Legendary Hour</a>, Kaidou was solemnly impressed by Oden's strength and willpower. As a last sign of respect for Oden, he informed the daimyo about Higurashi's demise while honestly apologizing to him for her meddling in their battle and opted to kill Oden himself with a gunshot.<sup id="cite_ref-c972p16_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c972p16-71">[71]</a></sup> Twenty years later, when CP0 member <a href="/wiki/Guernika" title="Guernika">Guernika</a> interfered and allowed him to win the fight between him and Luffy, he was horrified by what had happened and furiously smashed the agent despite their ongoing business relationship.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup> When Luffy revealed himself to have survived said interference, Kaidou was thankful for it and even apologized for what had happened previously, something which Luffy accepted.<sup id="cite_ref-c1044_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1044-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p><p>Outside of battle and fighting, however, Kaidou can be rather treacherous and opportunistic. He seemingly believes that betrayal is part of a pirate's nature and admitted that he overlooked the threat of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> because he never expected noble samurai to ally with pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> Kaidou is not above making false promises, having lied to Oden twice to keep the daimyo and his country in check. The first time, it was to buy time as Oden demoralized himself to Wano's citizens for years, allowing Kaidou to build more strength for his army. The second time was to have Oden and the Scabbards killed so the country would lose their hope of revolution, despite a prior agreement to spare them if they survived a certain punishment. Kaidou also has no qualms killing allies should they outlive their usefulness, having beheaded Orochi once the latter questioned his plot to reform Wano into a pirate paradise despite their alliance of over two decades.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou seems to have double standards when it comes to his property, as he was furious when <a href="/wiki/Fuga" title="Fuga">Fuga</a> stole and ate a SMILE from his room out of hunger, and had the artificial giant locked up for it,<sup id="cite_ref-Past_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Past-75">[75]</a></sup> but he seemed fine with <a href="/wiki/Ulti" title="Ulti">Ulti</a> stealing two Ancient Zoan Devil Fruits from him for herself and <a href="/wiki/Page_One" title="Page One">her brother</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs100_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs100-76">[76]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kaidou is determined to build <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">his crew</a> into the strongest army of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> users ready for what he has declared to be the biggest all-out war against the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. Thus, he actively sought out strong and formidable manpower in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> to draft into his ranks, from pirates such as the <a href="/wiki/Super_Rookie" title="Super Rookie">Super Rookies</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> to the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Mt._Atama_Thieves" title="Mt. Atama Thieves">Mt. Atama Thieves</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Shutenmaru</a>. Those who resist or defy his attempts are often sent to slave away at the <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">mines</a> of Udon until they either die or their spirits break and submit to his authority. As such, a great portion of the Beasts Pirates consists of former independent <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirates</a> who have given up their own goals in order to serve him.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou himself has not demonstrated much concern for the well-being of his crew, although he does seem to care about them to a degree, as <a href="/wiki/Scotch" title="Scotch">Scotch</a> stated that Kaidou would go after <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a> if the latter attacked him.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> Kaidou is invested in making his crew stronger by giving them artificial <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a> powers with <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> and, under his permission, incentivizes battles between his own crewmembers so they can attain higher ranks in his organization. When Kaidou gets drunk and emotional, he can get very violent against his subordinates and may end up smashing them around with <a href="/wiki/Hassaikai" title="Hassaikai">his kanabō</a>; although if he is in a good enough mood, he might just ignore them. Still, Kaidou's men tend to become concerned in those cases anyway, since their captain is known for rampaging around indiscriminately and causing damage to their own territories and facilities.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage-79">[79]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="King">King</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou has known <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a> for 34 years,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_2_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card_2-80">[80]</a></sup> with the two of them meeting as test subject prisoners on <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a> before the Beasts Pirates were formed; it appears that their union marked the beginning of the crew's formation. Kaidou appeared to be interested in King due to his strength, and when told of his original name "Arber", suggested he adopt the name King as a reflection of his status and power.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521102401" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou and King Talk About Joy Boy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou and King Talk About Joy Boy.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521102401"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521102401" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou and King Talk About Joy Boy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521102401" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou and King Talk About Joy Boy.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521102401"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_and_King_Talk_About_Joy_Boy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">King and Kaidou converse about Joy Boy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>King has been fiercely loyal to Kaidou ever since, believing in Kaidou's declaration that he was the only one who could change the world and declaring with great faith that Kaidou would become the next Pirate King.<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_King_meet_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_King_meet-46">[46]</a></sup> King also seemingly thought in the past that Kaidou could attain the identity of <a href="/wiki/Joy_Boy" title="Joy Boy">Joy Boy</a>. King expressed disbelief when Kaidou told him that Joy Boy would be the one to beat him because of his unwavering loyalty and belief in Kaidou's ambition. Eventually, King stopped caring about any comparisons with the legend.<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_King_and_Joy_Boy_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_King_and_Joy_Boy-47">[47]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> Kaidou took King with him on a ploy to kill Whitebeard before they were stopped by Shanks.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Queen">Queen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>33 years ago, Kaidou met Scien and offered him a position in his <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">pirate crew</a>, with the scientist accepting seven years later taking the name <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_2_80-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card_2-80">[80]</a></sup> Upon delivering the news of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Komurasaki</a>'s apparent death to Queen, Kaidou was unconcerned about Queen's feelings upon hearing this despite the All-Star being enamored with her, to the point of even mocking him for crying about it.<sup id="cite_ref-c941_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c941-83">[83]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack">Jack</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png/revision/latest?cb=20211212042428" class="image"><img alt="Jack Temporarily Incapacitated" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jack Temporarily Incapacitated.png" data-image-key="Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20211212042428"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png/revision/latest?cb=20211212042428" class="image"><img alt="Jack Temporarily Incapacitated" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20211212042428" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jack Temporarily Incapacitated.png" data-image-key="Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20211212042428"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jack_Temporarily_Incapacitated.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou saves Jack from Inuarashi and Nekomamushi in their Sulong forms.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As one of his All-Stars, Kaidou cares about Jack's well-being a great deal. When he heard about <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> failing to rescue <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, Kaidou was more concerned about the loss of his supply of SMILEs, though his lack of concern about Jack shows he never comes to question his wellbeing nor capacity as a fighter.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> When Jack was brutally beaten by <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> after the two <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">minks</a> activated their <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> forms, Kaidou intervened to save Jack's life. He held no grudge against Jack for being defeated, knowing that it was due to the minks' extreme strength rather than the All-Star's weakness; in fact, he even commended Jack for his work in keeping the other minks at bay and told him to get his wounds treated.<sup id="cite_ref-c991_68-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c991-68">[68]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tobiroppo">Tobiroppo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The Tobiroppo consist of the six strongest Shinuchi in the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>. Kaidou appears to be very proud of them, wishing to introduce them to his fellow <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a> and ally Big Mom. He also trusts them with missions dealing with his son <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>.
</p><p>The Tobiroppo seem to have the utmost respect for their captain. <a href="/wiki/Sasaki" title="Sasaki">Sasaki</a> shows interest in socializing solely with Kaidou, looking down on those in the lower ranks. <a href="/wiki/Black_Maria" title="Black Maria">Black Maria</a> acts in a flirty way towards her captain and appears to enjoy his company. <a href="/wiki/Who%27s-Who" title="Who's-Who">Who's-Who</a> is very loyal to his captain, as he was aware of X Drake's plans to betray their captain, and laid a trap of his own to expose him as a spy and traitor.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ulti_and_Page_One">Ulti and Page One</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou took the siblings <a href="/wiki/Ulti" title="Ulti">Ulti</a> and <a href="/wiki/Page_One" title="Page One">Page One</a> in after death of their father since Kaidou had been acquainted with him. Ulti eventually stole two Devil Fruits (Ryu Ryu no Mi, Models: <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Pachycephalosaurus" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Pachycephalosaurus">Pachycephalosaurus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ryu_Ryu_no_Mi,_Model:_Spinosaurus" title="Ryu Ryu no Mi, Model: Spinosaurus">Spinosaurus</a>) from Kaidou for herself and Page One to partake of, to make themselves into formidable fighting forces for Kaidou and thereby persevere in the Beasts Pirates, a crew in which only the strong survive.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup> Eventually, the siblings both became Tobiroppo. Ulti is not afraid of criticizing Kaidou's familial issues, much to the shock of her companions, but otherwise genuinely thinks that her boss will eventually become pirate king, enough to become massively angered towards anyone who dares to dispute that claim. Page One seems loyal and respectful to Kaidou, being heavily dismayed by his sister's brazenly casual, if not, at times, rude attitude toward him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou first met his fellow Emperor <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a>, better known as Big Mom, back when he was just 15 years old, right after joining the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> as an apprentice. Surprised by his young age, Linlin introduced herself to him and gave him advice to not trust Rocks, while declaring that she would rule the seas someday. During the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>, Linlin gifted the <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a> to Kaidou, granting him power in exchange for a life debt. Linlin has admitted that she sees Kaidou akin to a younger brother thanks to their time spent together in the crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c999p19_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c999p19-85">[85]</a></sup> In the aftermath of God Valley, Linlin showed genuine concern for Kaidou, worried of where he would go next in life without their crew around anymore. Kaidou, meanwhile, seems to hold a soft spot over their time as past crewmates, at least while drunk.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314035456" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Big Mom vs. Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314035456"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314035456" class="image"><img alt="Big Mom vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314035456" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Big Mom vs. Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e0/Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314035456"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou and Big Mom dueling.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nowadays, both of them would like nothing more than to kill each other. Kaidou does not hold respect for Big Mom and calls her an "old hag". When Big Mom contacted him about allowing her to kill Luffy in Wano, he refused to oblige and threatened to kill her if she dared to enter his territory no matter the reason, not caring about Linlin claiming that he owed her a debt.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-66">[66]</a></sup> When hearing Big Mom came to Wano, Kaidou ordered his troops to sink her ship before they have an all-out war. However, Kaidou does not wish to kill Big Mom in an underhanded manner. Rather, when he was given an opportunity to do so after she was captured and brought to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, he preferred to engage her in equal combat, ordering his subordinates to release her from her <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> chains and kept his promise that he would kill her since she came to Wano before their fight.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup>
</p><p>However, following their battle, Kaidou and Big Mom found common ground in their shared, former dream of world domination and temporarily put aside their differences in order to achieve said dream. Having reignited their sibling bond, they now act quite jovially around each other as they drank and were excited about working together again, although they ultimately still wished to kill each other once they accomplished their goals, as they have claimed.<sup id="cite_ref-c954_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c954-87">[87]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou and Big Mom have a very vitriolic attitude towards each other while fighting side by side, trading insults and pointing out behaviors they perceive as annoying coming from the other, like Big Mom showing irritation at Kaidou's habit of taking attacks head-on to test the strength of his adversaries. That being said, they have great combat synergy and are considered unbeatable together, to the point that the Super Rookies from the Worst Generation fighting them had to devise a plan to separate the two in order to stand a chance. Kaidou and Big Mom are also capable of performing a formidable combination technique, <i>Hakai</i>, that is capable of decimating everything in their way. When Kaidou sensed that Big Mom was actually defeated, he was genuinely upset, as he remembered the sibling like bond they formed during their time in the Rocks Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou and <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> had a business partnership where Doflamingo supplied Kaidou with <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE fruits</a> created by <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> in exchange for weapons, which he significantly invested in his goal to make his crew the strongest of Devil Fruit users. Word of Doflamingo's defeat and the destruction of the <a href="/wiki/SMILE_Factory" title="SMILE Factory">SMILE factory</a> brought Kaidou mourning at his loss much to his drunken emotional sorrow.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</a> later states that Kaidou would have killed Doflamingo if he ceased producing SMILE, and Doflamingo became very fearful at the possibility of incurring Kaidou's wrath when Luffy and Law threatened his production.<sup id="cite_ref-Joker's_worry_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Joker's_worry-63">[63]</a></sup> Despite calling him weak, Kaidou heavily valued Doflamingo's business to the degree that when Doflamingo was captured by the Marines, he ordered <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> to stop hunting for one of the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Kouzuki Family's retainers</a> and to free Doflamingo from an armada of <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">Marine warships</a> escorting him to <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Yamato">Yamato</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231011091225" class="image"><img alt="Yamato Clashes with Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Yamato Clashes with Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011091225"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231011091225" class="image"><img alt="Yamato Clashes with Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011091225" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Yamato Clashes with Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231011091225"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Yamato_Clashes_with_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou clashes with his son, Yamato.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a> is Kaidou's son, born as his daughter, and only known blood relative. The two of them have a strained relationship, as Yamato idolizes Kaidou's enemy, Oden, a fact that drove multiple conflicts between the two. However, Yamato still emulated Oden for the past 20 years to the point of even presenting himself as a man like him, and although Kaidou disapproves of his idolizing him, he does refer to Yamato as his "son". Kaidou does not seem to be aware that Yamato wishes to fulfill Oden's dream of opening Wano's borders, a cause to which he is opposed.<sup id="cite_ref-daughter_Yamato_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-daughter_Yamato-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;"><b>Kaidou</b>: Orochi had a skill for exploitation.   <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>

  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
Kaidou has been cruel to Yamato ever since his childhood. When Kaidou first learned of Yamato's desire to be like Oden, he imprisoned him inside a dark cave without any food and with other samurai that held a grudge against him, putting the child in direct danger. It was this event that led Yamato to become Kaidou's enemy, intending to fight him in the promised time, according to Oden's <a href="/wiki/Logbook#Kouzuki_Oden's_Logbook" title="Logbook">logbook</a>. Along the years, Kaidou beat Yamato numerous times, keeping his life in precarious conditions through explosive handcuffs, which prevented him from simply sneaking away by setting sail, and frequent hunger, driving Yamato to eat one of Kaidou's valuable <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Inu_Inu_no_Mi,_Model:_Okuchi_no_Makami" title="Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Okuchi no Makami">Inu Inu no Mi, Model: Okuchi no Makami</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup> Kaidou's overall view of Yamato is contradictory; he casually refers to him as an "idiot" but wished to have him participate in his party during the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Fire Festival</a><sup id="cite_ref-c977_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c977-20">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c979_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c979-21">[21]</a></sup> and later even replace Orochi as shogun, being confident that Yamato would eventually follow his will and protect Wano under his rule.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup> When Kaidou finally confronted Yamato during the <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> Raid, he continuously mocked his son for attempting to rebel against him by allying with the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">enemy alliance</a>, forcefully telling him to stay in Wano and become its guardian.
</p><p>In return, Yamato seems to have a very low opinion of his father and has claimed to have attempted to defeat him multiple times in the past in order to attain freedom, being particularly frustrated about the explosive handcuffs that would detonate if he attempted to escape. He sought <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> precisely to join forces with him in order to take down Kaidou and did not object to the idea of Luffy defeating him. Yamato was noticeably angry when Kaidou announced his plans to have him become the next shogun of Wano, which showed signs that he did not wish to be his father's pawn like Orochi was. 
</p><p>Initially, Yamato was not so sure if Kaidou was really willing to kill his own son and believed that the explosive handcuffs was just a bluff. Once Yamato realized that his father was true to his word (after Luffy removed his handcuffs), he officially disowned him as his parent and did not even appear to care if he were to die during the raid on Onigashima, becoming intent on cutting any remaining ties they once had. This is reflected by Yamato, after being freed from his handcuffs, referring to Kaidou by name instead of "father".<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Family">Kouzuki Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou became mortal enemies with the Kouzuki Family, as he worked with Orochi to kill Oden and caused <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Toki" title="Kouzuki Toki">Kouzuki Toki</a>'s death while attempting to kill her and her children, <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Hiyori" title="Kouzuki Hiyori">Kouzuki Hiyori</a>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Oden">Kouzuki Oden</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ef/Tougen_Totsuka.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726055921" class="image"><img alt="Tougen Totsuka" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tougen Totsuka.png" data-image-key="Tougen_Totsuka.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ef/Tougen_Totsuka.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210726055921"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ef/Tougen_Totsuka.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726055921" class="image"><img alt="Tougen Totsuka" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ef/Tougen_Totsuka.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210726055921" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tougen Totsuka.png" data-image-key="Tougen_Totsuka.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ef/Tougen_Totsuka.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210726055921"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tougen_Totsuka.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Oden injures Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the first person to have ever injured him, Oden left a deep, strong impression on Kaidou. Kaidou thought highly of Oden, having heard of the samurai's infamous reputation prior to their actual meeting, to the point of prioritizing the gradual expansion of his army to properly tackle the Kuri daimyo. Impressed by the man's feat of surviving a boiling pot of oil <a href="/wiki/Legendary_Hour" title="Legendary Hour">for a whole hour</a>, Kaidou decided to kill Oden himself as a sign of respect, acknowledging that his enemy had died as a legend. Before executing him, Kaidou coldly apologized to Oden for <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Higurashi" title="Kurozumi Higurashi">Kurozumi Higurashi</a>'s interference and revealed to the daimyo that he has the "old hag" killed as punishment.
</p><p>In spite of Oden's death ever since, Kaidou still seems to be haunted by his fight with him, particularly the fact that he could have died that day if it were not for Higurashi's actions. When the Nine Red Scabbards ambushed him during the raid on Onigashima, he was shocked to see Oden's image in them, reminiscent of how he was nearly defeated by their master twenty years ago. When the Scabbards successfully injured him, the scar he received from Oden started hurting to the point he screamed in agony. Later on, after finally evaluating the Scabbards' strength during their fight at the top of the Skull Dome, Kaidou concluded that, in spite of carrying Oden's will, the Scabbards would never be able to measure to their fallen master, with the Emperor even claiming that it was an impossible task for any samurai.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kouzuki_Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20230205233816" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Threatens Momonosuke" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou Threatens Momonosuke.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230205233816"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png/revision/latest?cb=20230205233816" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Threatens Momonosuke" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230205233816" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou Threatens Momonosuke.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230205233816"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_Threatens_Momonosuke.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou threatens to kill Momonosuke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the past, Kaidou threatened to kill Momonosuke, holding him by the throat above the Kuri Castle when Momonosuke declared his ambition to be the shogun. Kaidou considered him an immature brat in response, knowing that the boy was only speaking out of duty rather than actual ambition. Considering him as pathetic compared to his father, Kaidou chose to leave Momonosuke behind in the burning castle rather than kill him personally. This experience has ever since caused Momonosuke to be afraid of heights, refusing to fly despite that being within his capabilities while in dragon form.
</p><p>Because of Kaidou's actions, Momonosuke and his retainers wish to bring him down after being sent 20 years forward in time by Toki and have spent all their time working to form an alliance to accomplish this.<sup id="cite_ref-c920_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920-93">[93]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup> When Kaidou first saw Momonosuke again after twenty years, he remained unimpressed upon seeing him brutally beaten by Kanjuro. He also questioned Momonosuke whether he was truly Oden's son, claiming that he did not inherit any of his father's strength and guts, which Kaidou thought highly of. Repeating the question he asked twenty years ago, Kaidou offered to spare Momonosuke if he denied about his heritage. When Momonosuke refused to lie, Kaidou prepared to execute him as a Kouzuki in order to officially start his New Onigashima Project. After Luffy's rematch with Kaidou which ended in the former's second loss, Kaidou personally hunted down Momonosuke, and brutally injured Kin'emon his guardian, causing Momonosuke to cry profusely. When Momonosuke flew to Onigashima as an adult Dragon, Kaidou was surprised while also claiming only one Dragon is allowed to exist.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nine_Red_Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>To fulfill Oden's wish of opening <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano</a>'s borders, the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Scabbards</a> (except <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</a>, who was a traitor) plotted to defeat Kaidou. Ten years before Momonosuke's return, <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> gave up hope after his comrades became impatient and perished trying to fight the Beasts Pirates. Kaidou was impressed with Ashura's strength and wanted him to join his crew. Although he had stopped following the Kouzuki Family, Ashura had no wish to serve Kaidou and refused, though Kaidou remained open to him joining and offered to forgive Ashura if he did.<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage-79">[79]</a></sup> However, after <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> sacrificed himself to give the Kouzuki revolution a chance, Ashura eventually rejoined the Kouzuki Family and their quest to bring down Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> Kaidou was shocked to learn that most of them survived and were in the future, and was surprised to hear Kanjuro, whom he had nearly killed twenty years ago, was in reality, a secret ally of Orochi and was very impressed by Kanjuro for his deceptive skill that had also fooled him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231121020441"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20231121020441" class="image"><img alt="Scabbards Attack Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231121020441" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Scabbards Attack Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a5/Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231121020441"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Scabbards_Attack_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Scabbards attack Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
