<p>The remaining Scabbards, bearing twenty years of anger and hatred over their master's death, eventually succeeded in ambushing him during the Fire Festival, with another of Oden's retainers, <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> by their side. Kaidou was surprised to learn that Kyoshiro is actually <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a> and Ashura Doji was a member as well. Despite proudly claiming that they could never hurt him, Kaidou envisioned Oden's angry image commanding he leave Wano and never return as they furiously attacked him, pushing him off his feet. When the Scabbards actually injured Kaidou and made him scream in pain, he went serious enough to take the battle outside of the Skull Dome with the Scabbards.<sup id="cite_ref-c987_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c987-96">[96]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite continuing his claims that they would not be able to harm him, Kaidou was shocked and impressed with the Scabbards resolve, he even told Jack and his men to leave so he could fight them all alone, as he saw that Jack was close to being killed by the Mink rulers <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> after they entered their <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> forms. From that point, Kaidou battled all nine of the Samurai and was impressed that <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin'emon">two</a> <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">were</a> able repel and redirect his attacks, while <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">another</a> <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">three</a> <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">attacked</a> him head-on, and the Mink rulers attacked ferociously as well. Kaidou was amazed that their attacks were actually harming him and was even left stunned when <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin'emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura</a>, and even Inuarashi managed to strike him down together with the exact same move that Oden used to permanently scar him, in the exact same spot that Oden scarred him, opening the wound back up. Despite this accomplishment, however, Kaidou saw this as the extent of their combined skills, getting back up and telling them that the cut was still too shallow, stating that their attacks while injuring him could not compare to Oden. He then went on to ruthlessly defeat all nine of the Samurai, and left them severely beaten, seemingly disappointed that none of them could measure up to Oden in the end. After fighting with members of the Worst Generation on the roof alongside Big Mom, Kaidou returned to the Skull Dome to kill Momonosuke, and was both annoyed and impressed by the samurai's continued attempts to stop him, even commending Kin'emon for protecting his master, before striking him down for the second time.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gol_D._Roger">Gol D. Roger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou considered <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> his enemy for at least 38 years prior to present, as on his arrival at <a href="/wiki/God_Valley" title="God Valley">God Valley</a> Kaidou alluded to a previous confrontation before being cut off by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a>. Shortly after he, his former captain <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</a>, Linlin and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> engaged in combat with Roger and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a>'s alliance, this event would go on to be labeled as the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a> and end in Rocks' death and the dissolution of the crew, with Kaidou going his separate way afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup> Kaidou appeared to respect Roger's strength highly enough to consider him one of the few people capable of fighting him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1001_98-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1001-98">[98]</a></sup> Even though Kaidou referred to Roger as soft, <sup id="cite_ref-c970p5_99-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970p5-99">[99]</a></sup> he believed his rise to Pirate King was genuinely well earned as he managed to conquer the seas purely with <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a> and without a Devil Fruit, giving Kaidou the belief that only Haki can "transcend all".<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Edward_Newgate">Edward Newgate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Much like with Big Mom, the late <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> was Kaidou's fellow Emperor and former crewmate on the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>. While acknowledging and respecting him for his power, Kaidou viewed <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> as too soft because of his morals and honor code.<sup id="cite_ref-c970p5_99-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970p5-99">[99]</a></sup> He also considered Whitebeard as one of the few powerful individuals capable of fighting him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1001_98-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1001-98">[98]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Prior to the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, Kaidou and King attempted to intercept Whitebeard while he was on his way to <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> with the intention of killing him, although the attempt was stopped by <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-VsShanks_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VsShanks-42">[42]</a></sup> Two years later, he cursed Whitebeard for being able to die while he was unable to.<sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Not much is known about the relationship between Kaidou and Shanks, but when Kaidou attempted to attack Whitebeard, Shanks personally intervened and stopped him from doing so. Kaidou seems to acknowledge Shanks' abilities, considering him among the few powerful individuals capable of fighting him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1001_98-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1001-98">[98]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Worst_Generation">Worst Generation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As a member of the Four Emperors, Kaidou serves as an obstacle for members of the Worst Generation in their quest to obtain the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Kaidou first heard of Luffy after finding out that he had worked with Law to destroy the SMILE production. Kaidou refused to consider Luffy a serious threat, viewing him defeating Doflamingo as nothing special.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> However, he still held a grudge over Luffy for his actions in <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a>, swearing revenge on the Straw Hat captain for ruining his <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> deal with the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> and telling Big Mom that he would kill the boy himself for it.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_66-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-66">[66]</a></sup> 
</p><p>When Kaidou heard about Luffy and Law's presence in <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, he personally went to the <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> region to demand that his subordinate <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> search for and capture them as fast as possible. Kaidou eventually fought Luffy shortly after and, although he defeated the Straw Hat captain in one hit, he was impressed by his fighting talent and ordered the boy's imprisonment, wishing to break the young pirate's spirit and have him as a soldier within his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c924_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924-34">[34]</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Luffy_Among_Legends.png/revision/latest?cb=20220511175113" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Among Legends" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="153" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Among Legends.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Among_Legends.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Luffy_Among_Legends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220511175113"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Luffy_Among_Legends.png/revision/latest?cb=20220511175113" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Among Legends" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Luffy_Among_Legends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220511175113" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="153" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Among Legends.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Among_Legends.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Luffy_Among_Legends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220511175113"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Among_Legends.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou imagines Luffy among the ranks of legendary pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>, once they finally fought again, Kaidou was shocked that Luffy had managed to learn a method to penetrate his defenses, mentally comparing him to other big names of pirate history: Roger, Whitebeard, Oden, Shanks, and his former captain, Rocks. Kaidou was also impressed that Luffy was not going down as easily as in their first encounter, praising the young pirate for properly defending himself against some of his stronger attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> Kaidou overall grew more and more amused with Luffy's spirit, thrill for battle, and quick growth the more they fought, seemingly acknowledging the Straw Hat captain as a worthy opponent akin to Oden. This is further evidenced by the fact that Kaidou regretted not having killed Luffy in a more definitive way once the latter was knocked off of Onigashima, as not doing so meant he would be unable to truly crush the spirits of everyone that had deposited their faith into Luffy's survival and victory.
</p><p>After Luffy returned to Onigashima and displayed his better control over his Supreme King Haki by dealing more damage to him, Kaidou remarked having a good time fighting him, enough to resort to his <i>Shuron Hakke</i> style, considered by him an admission that he was taking Luffy seriously. Kaidou, however, became devastated when the lead <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> agent Guernika intentionally sabotaged their duel, as it reminded him of how his fight with Oden ended. Fortunately for Kaidou, Luffy was able to recover after his Devil Fruit awakened. Kaidou even apologized to Luffy for Guernika's interference.
</p><p>During their next fight, Kaidou continued to thoroughly enjoy fighting Luffy due to him being one of the most challenging and interesting opponents that he had ever faced. While he remained convinced that Luffy could not change the world, he was still curious as to what type of world Luffy wanted to create. After Luffy won their clash, Kaidou recalled a previous conversation he had with King where he stated that Joy Boy would be the one to defeat him, implying that in his final moments, he acknowledged that Luffy was Joy Boy after all and that he had finally met his end.<sup id="cite_ref-c1049_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1049-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy viewed Kaidou as one of his biggest obstacles in the way of his goal of becoming the Pirate King, having stated several times that he wished to bring him down as well as the other Four Emperors. In Wano, Luffy learned from <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin'emon">Kin'emon</a> about the tragedy that befell the country after Kaidou and Orochi took over, having witnessed firsthand the suffering Kaidou had brought to the people of Wano, particularly <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Tama" title="Kurozumi Tama">Tama</a>, who he had befriended and promised a better life to once the Beasts Pirates were gone. Once Kaidou came to Kuri and targeted Luffy's crew, the latter grew outraged and quickly engaged the Emperor in combat but was no match for him. After getting incarcerated at the <a href="/wiki/Prisoner_Mine" title="Prisoner Mine">Prisoner Mine</a> and swearing payback, Luffy trained himself extensively in order to obtain enough power to truly injure Kaidou.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Roronoa_Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20220802050119" class="image"><img alt="Zoro Cuts Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="198" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zoro Cuts Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220802050119"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20220802050119" class="image"><img alt="Zoro Cuts Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220802050119" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="198" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zoro Cuts Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/34/Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220802050119"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zoro_Cuts_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou permanently scarred for the first time in decades by Zoro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, who seeks to be the World's Greatest Swordsman, once declared that he wanted to fight the World's Strongest Creature. As such, Zoro assisted Luffy during the fight against Kaidou and his wielding of Oden's former sword, <a href="/wiki/Enma" title="Enma">Enma</a>, caught the Emperor's attention, who had detected the familiar Haki emanating from it. Like the other members of the Worst Generation involved in the fight, Kaidou praised Zoro's strength. Kaidou was extremely shocked when Zoro somehow managed to channel Supreme King Haki to slash him across the torso, acknowledging that the Pirate Hunter had been able to replicate Oden's feat from two decades ago.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Trafalgar_D._Water_Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Law was aware of Kaidou's deal with Doflamingo and used this knowledge to forge an alliance with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, knowing that Luffy would attempt to take down the Four Emperors. Law used Kaidou's threat in order to force Doflamingo's hand and have the Warlord and Dressrosa ruler resign from his position, as part of his personal revenge plan against his former boss. With Doflamingo's defeat, Law continued with his original scheme to take down Kaidou alongside the Straw Hats.
</p><p>As with Luffy, Kaidou became enemies with Law after finding out that the two pirates had destroyed his SMILE production. Like Luffy, Kaidou wants to kill Law, but does not consider him to be a real threat.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> He went to Kuri to apprehend them upon finding out they were present in Wano, but after defeating Luffy, Kaidou postponed his search for Law.<sup id="cite_ref-c924_34-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c924-34">[34]</a></sup> During the raid on Onigashima, Kaidou grew to respect Law's strength, particularly his usage of the <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">Ope Ope no Mi</a>, which Kaidou had trouble defending against.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Eustass_Kid">Eustass Kid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Eustass Kid encountered Kaidou when the latter fell out of the sky and landed at the <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a>' hideout before coming face to face with the rookie pirate. Kid refused to submit to Kaidou and tried to fight him only to be defeated and captured. Kaidou then imprisoned Kid, hoping to eventually break his spirit. 
</p><p>During his imprisonment, Kid held a strong grudge against Kaidou and firmly told Luffy that he would be the one to defeat the Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> However, after seeing what happened to <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a>, Kid decided to prioritize finding the rest of his crew and rejected Luffy's offer for an alliance. After getting his crew back, he joined Luffy and Law to take down Kaidou. However, Kid only did so for the glory of defeating him, not to support the Kouzuki revolution.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="X_Drake">X Drake</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Upon entering the New World, X Drake immediately sought to join Kaidou's crew, going as far as to attack <a href="/wiki/Scotch" title="Scotch">one of his trusted subordinates</a> on one of his favorite islands just to get his attention. He eventually succeeded and became one of his highest-ranking officers, a Tobiroppo. He carried out many duties in Kaidou's name, such as quelling an uprising on the island he himself attacked and captured the <a href="/wiki/Caribou" title="Caribou">instigator</a> responsible, as well as hunting down <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and those bearing the mark of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a>'s rebellion.
</p><p>In truth, however, Drake was still a member of the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, specifically their <a href="/wiki/SWORD" title="SWORD">SWORD</a> branch. He seemingly intended to sabotage Kaidou while the <a href="/wiki/Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai_Alliance" title="Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance">Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance</a> launched their attack on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, having freed one of the alliance's leaders, Law, some days prior to the raid and attempting to get rid of Queen, one of Kaidou's All-Stars, alongside Who's-Who. When the latter situation turned out to be a trap though, Drake found himself with no choice but to switch sides and join the alliance.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Scratchmen_Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Scratchmen Apoo was one of Kaidou's esteemed informants. It was through the longarm that Kaidou managed to locate Eustass Kid and <a href="/wiki/Basil_Hawkins" title="Basil Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</a> in order to recruit them into his crew, as well as receive updates about Jack's well-being after <a href="/wiki/Zunesha" title="Zunesha">Zunesha</a> managed to sink him. They held a generally casual relationship, with Kaidou actually getting surprised, but not negatively, about Apoo returning to Wano for the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Festival" title="Fire Festival">Golden Kagura</a> festivities, which the latter greatly enjoyed. 
</p><p>That being said, Apoo was not loyal to Kaidou at all and planned to take the Emperor out should he had won his duel with Luffy. Apoo also had no problem reporting CP0's deals with Kaidou, which could have jeopardized their business relations.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Basil_Hawkins">Basil Hawkins</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Hawkins is one of the members of the Worst Generation that Kaidou had successfully managed to recruit by force. Unlike Kid, who kept fighting Kaidou to the end, Hawkins submitted himself to the Emperor due to having no other choice according to his fortune-telling, with Kaidou gladly welcoming him into his ranks.
</p><p>Despite regretting his choice and actually foreseeing Kaidou's eventual defeat during the Raid on Onigashima, Hawkins remained loyal to the Emperor mostly out of personal pride, as he thought he had no right to switch sides after witnessing Kid's defiance.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Family">Kurozumi Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou originally worked alongside the <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a> in order to monopolize the Wano Country. However, Kaidou was merely using them to further his ends, and upon revealing the <a href="/wiki/New_Onigashima_Project" title="New Onigashima Project">New Onigashima Project</a>, he ultimately betrayed them.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Higurashi">Kurozumi Higurashi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230917031716" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Higurashi Proposition" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou Higurashi Proposition.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230917031716"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png/revision/latest?cb=20230917031716" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Higurashi Proposition" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230917031716" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou Higurashi Proposition.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230917031716"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_Higurashi_Proposition.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Higurashi approaching Kaidou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Higurashi" title="Kurozumi Higurashi">Kurozumi Higurashi</a> was the one who approached Kaidou to propose an alliance between him and her family 28 years ago; he would help them take complete control of the Wano Country in exchange for powerful weapons.
</p><p>Higurashi also aided Kaidou in his fight against Oden by posing as a captive Momonosuke, thus allowing Kaidou to deal a finishing blow. But this proved to be a costly mistake, as Kaidou despised those who would interfere in his fights, and killed her as punishment. He even apologized to Oden for her interfearance prior to killing him.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kurozumi_Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314031836" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Decapitates Orochi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaidou Decapitates Orochi.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314031836"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230314031836" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Decapitates Orochi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314031836" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaidou Decapitates Orochi.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230314031836"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaidou_Decapitates_Orochi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou beheads Orochi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, the shogun of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>, had been allies for over 25 years after Orochi bought his loyalty using the money previously borrowed from Oden.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup> Their bond appeared to be strong, as Kaidou would attack anyone who threatened Orochi,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup> and Orochi was extremely confident in having Kaidou's support, which allowed him to do anything, including opposing the World Government and exploiting them for his own gains.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup> They were friendly enough to share drinks together in Orochi's castle. Kaidou was initially dismissive about Orochi's warning of the Kouzuki Family's comeback and even poked fun at Orochi's paranoia. Nevertheless, when Orochi had proven information from his spy Kanjuro, Kaidou chose to believe Orochi, instructing the latter not to kill the time travelers as he wished to ask them information regarding Oden's journey to <a href="/wiki/Laugh_Tale" title="Laugh Tale">Laugh Tale</a>. When he saw the broadcast of Orochi killing <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Shimotsuki Yasuie</a> and the false laughter of the crowd watching, Kaidou expressed amusement at the shogun's cruelty.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the end though, Kaidou was merely using Orochi as a pawn, and once Kaidou revealed his New Onigashima Project, he beheaded Orochi when the latter objected to it.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup> Kaidou complimented Orochi's skill in exploitation, as the latter was the one who transformed Wano into a weapons factory for the former, but otherwise saw the former shogun as expendable in that role and wanted his own son Yamato to take over.<sup id="cite_ref-c1020_90-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1020-90">[90]</a></sup> Unbeknownst to Kaidou, Orochi managed to survive from his beheading and became murderously furious towards Kaidou for betraying him.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ever since he was a child, Kaidou was unreserved about his feelings towards the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. Having been used as a bargaining chip to allow his homeland a spot in the <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>, Kaidou held resentment towards the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> and their absolute rights. As such, Kaidou sought to drag them down from power and into the battlefield, following his own ideals of freedom and equality.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup> Whenever Kaidou was hungry, he would allow himself to be arrested only to eat all the rations within the area before escaping, much to the Marines' annoyance.
</p><p>One of the reasons Kaidou made deals with Doflamingo and joined forces with Big Mom was to attain enough military might to tackle the World Government. His conquest of Wano was also part of those plans, since the country's geography made it a favorable territory for an eventual war. As noted by Admiral <a href="/wiki/Aramaki" title="Aramaki">Ryokugyu</a>, not even the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> dared to invade Wano as long as Kaidou was present, as the combination between the Emperor's forces and the island's natural defenses created a powerful deterrent to the government's interest in taking over the country. Still, paradoxically enough, Kaidou was not against making trading weapons with the government itself in order to obtain their military assets and build up further power, using Orochi and Doflamingo as intermediaries for those deals.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230730030111" class="image"><img alt="Guernika Facing Kaidou" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Guernika Facing Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230730030111"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png/revision/latest?cb=20230730030111" class="image"><img alt="Guernika Facing Kaidou" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230730030111" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Guernika Facing Kaidou.png" data-image-key="Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0c/Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230730030111"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Guernika_Facing_Kaidou.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou attacks Guernika for his interference.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the government's representatives in Wano, Kaidou did not mind having CP0 as guests during the Golden Kagura. The CP0 agents initially preferred to remain as mere observers of the eventual raid, citing that both sides losing soldiers was a good thing, but eventually had to involve themselves in the fight after further orders were given. One of CP0's agents, Guernika, was even tasked with getting in the way of Luffy's duel with Kaidou, immediately understanding that it was essentially a suicide mission due to the Emperor's infamous hatred of interference during one-on-one combat. True enough, when said agent did manage to sabotage Luffy, a shocked and distraught Kaidou had no qualms in fatally smashing him despite their status as business partners. While apologizing to Luffy, Kaidou called Guernika as an "idiot".<sup id="cite_ref-c1044_69-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1044-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Others">Others</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rocks_D._Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou's former captain during his time as an <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Apprentice" title="Pirate Apprentice">apprentice</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>. The details of their relationship are unknown, but Kaidou seems to hold <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Xebec</a> in high regard and respects him for his strength.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Citizens">Wano Country Citizens</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou is said to be revered in Wano as a "wise king" and protector of their realm, although this only seems to be the case among people who are loyal to Orochi.<sup id="cite_ref-wise_king_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wise_king-12">[12]</a></sup> Anyone who becomes an enemy of Orochi also becomes an enemy of Kaidou. As such, he attacked and killed the remaining daimyo for their rebellion<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup> and attempted to kill the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> and everyone associated with it. Thus, Kouzuki Family loyalists consider Kaidou to be an enemy, and those who have allied with the family's survivors are working to take down Kaidou as well as Orochi.<sup id="cite_ref-c920_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920-93">[93]</a></sup> When Kaidou attempted to search <a href="/wiki/Kuri" title="Kuri">Kuri</a> for Luffy and Law while drunk, he mindlessly caused damage to <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Okobore_Town" title="Kuri">Okobore Town</a> without a second thought by flying through it.<sup id="cite_ref-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage_79-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kaidou_Drunk_Rampage-79">[79]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Kaidou announced the <a href="/wiki/New_Onigashima_Project" title="New Onigashima Project">New Onigashima Project</a>, he revealed that he had plans to enslave all of Wano's citizens, including those residing in the <a href="/wiki/Flower_Capital" title="Flower Capital">Flower Capital</a>, to have them make weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-c985_25-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c985-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">People often say "If it's one-on-one, Kaidou will win." On land, sea, and air... among all living things, he is a pirate who is known as the "strongest creature"!!!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Ending narration of Kaidou's introduction.<sup id="cite_ref-c795_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c795-110">[110]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
As one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>, Kaidou was recognized as one of the four most powerful pirates in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-Four_Emperors_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Four_Emperors-5">[5]</a></sup> famed as the world's <b>"Strongest Creature"</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-Strongest_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Strongest-11">[11]</a></sup> Notably, he has a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>4,611,100,000,<sup id="cite_ref-bounty_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-14">[14]</a></sup> which is the highest known bounty of any pirate currently alive and third highest in history, surpassed only by the bounties of the late <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>. As the Beasts Pirates' Governor-General, Kaidou has authority over a massive, 20,000-strong pirate organization, and due to his alliance with <a href="/wiki/Shogun" title="Shogun">Shogun</a> <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>, he and his crew enjoy authority over and cooperation with thousands of <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurai</a> forces serving Orochi. Even during his time as a kid and during his teenage years as a pirate apprentice with the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>, Kaidou was already formidable and, after his captain's fall and the crew's disintegration, only grew stronger throughout his life. 
</p><p>Kaidou attempted to take Whitebeard's life, something very few would dare, and subsequently had an encounter with <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-VsShanks_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VsShanks-42">[42]</a></sup> and a clash against <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> two years later.<sup id="cite_ref-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou-111">[111]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> also acknowledged Kaidou's strength. <a href="/wiki/Shepherd_Ju_Peter" title="Shepherd Ju Peter">St. Shepherd Ju Peter</a> stated that Kaidou was one of the few people capable of stopping <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Teach</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> and the five questioned themselves if angering Kaidou was worth preventing Luffy from awakening <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">his Devil Fruit</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> His strength was also recognized by his fellow Emperor Big Mom, who could not fathom the idea of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> defeating him.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup>
</p><p>According to <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>, Kaidou could easily kill <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, a world-famous, extremely powerful pirate in his own right; Doflamingo himself, despite his normally always-retained fearlessness, was visibly distressed at the prospect of angering Kaidou.<sup id="cite_ref-Joker's_worry_63-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Joker's_worry-63">[63]</a></sup> Additionally, Law speculated that his crew, the <a href="/wiki/Heart_Pirates" title="Heart Pirates">Heart Pirates</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> allied together would only have a roughly 30% chance of bringing down Kaidou,<sup id="cite_ref-c697p2_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c697p2-19">[19]</a></sup> though the statement is questionable seeing as at that time, Law was not serious about fighting him.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup> Kaidou defeated two other members of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Killer" title="Killer">Killer</a>, along with the rest of their <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">crew</a>, with seemingly no issue<sup id="cite_ref-c824p13_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824p13-55">[55]</a></sup> and refused to take Law and Luffy's alliance seriously regardless of their victory over Doflamingo, viewing defeating a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> as nothing special.<sup id="cite_ref-c920_93-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c920-93">[93]</a></sup> Kaidou's confidence was later proven to be warranted when he defeated Luffy with a single blow during their first fight. Before the fight on the rooftop of the <a href="/wiki/Skull_Dome" title="Skull Dome">Skull Dome</a> even began, Kaidou was convinced that only Gol D. Roger, Whitebeard, Kouzuki Oden, Shanks, and <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">his late captain</a> were capable of fighting him seriously.
</p><p>Overall, Kaidou has been said to have only lost eight battles in his lifetime and has only been injured twice. As stated during his introduction, people consider it a certainty for Kaidou to win any one-on-one battle he takes part in, and even most groups and armies have little ability to take him down. When the daimyos of Wano Country and the Kouzuki loyalists rebelled, Kaidou crushed them, and when hundreds of samurai went to <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> to attack Kaidou 10 years ago, they were all killed. He faced the <a href="/wiki/Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Nine Red Scabbards">Nine Red Scabbards</a> (except for <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kurozumi Kanjuro</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a> (a former commander of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>) by himself, and although he was having issues dealing with them in his dragon form, he easily overpowered all while in his human form (including <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a> form, whose strength at that time surpassed one of his <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates#All-Stars" title="Beasts Pirates">All-Stars</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>). Kaidou also took on the <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Pirates" title="Gecko Pirates">Gecko Pirates</a> 23 years ago and slaughtered all of them except for their captain, <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-First_Mention_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-First_Mention-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p><p>Similar to the other Emperors, Kaidou has many underlings and other pirate crews allied with him<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup> and can claim self-governing islands as his territories.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup> With <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> and Doflamingo as his associates, Kaidou created an army of over 500 <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">Artificial Zoan-type Devil Fruit</a> users, known as the Gifters.<sup id="cite_ref-c689_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c689-118">[118]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Even without his <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a>-type Devil Fruit powers, Kaidou is legendary for his supreme physical power as the world's <b>"Strongest Creature"</b>. With a one-handed swing of his kanabō, he can send normal-sized people flying into the distance,<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup> and he broke past the tremendous defensive power of Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques"><b>Gear 4</b></a> with great ease. He once sunk nine enormous prison ships singlehandedly.<sup id="cite_ref-Toughness_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toughness-119">[119]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> once said that even as a mere apprentice in the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>, Kaidou was able to earn the respect of his vicious companions through his strength alone.
</p><p>Most remarkably, Kaidou's body is nigh-indestructible far more that his former crewmate and fellow Emperor Big Mom, and even attacks strengthened by ordinary <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> cannot damage his incredibly tough defense. He took multiple powerful hits from Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques"><b>Gear 3</b></a> while in his dragon form and transformed back into his human form after being pummeled into the ground and proceeded to receive a barrage of Gear 4 hits that were even more powerful yet only became sober and felt nothing more than annoyance, received no injuries, and was able to quickly get back up and counterattack without issue.<sup id="cite_ref-c923_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c923-120">[120]</a></sup> This all changed once Luffy learned how to emit his Armament Haki and attack his enemy's insides during his training while in <a href="/wiki/Udon" title="Udon">Udon</a>, making Kaidou bleed with his newest <b>Gear 3</b> technique, which used advanced-grade Armament Haki,<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup> yet the damage inflicted was still "too shallow" according to Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> 
</p><p>While the Red Scabbards were able to accomplish the rare feat of drawing blood from him with their swords and attacks, these wounds had very little, if any, effect on him.<sup id="cite_ref-c987_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c987-96">[96]</a></sup> He could withstand having his own immensely destructive Bolo Breath redirected at him by <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Maki_Maki_no_Mi" title="Maki Maki no Mi">Maki Maki no Mi</a>, as well as assaults from Nekomamushi and Inuarashi's Sulong-enhanced attacks, <a href="/wiki/Kawamatsu" title="Kawamatsu">Kawamatsu</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Kappa_Style#Techniques" title="Kappa Style"><i>Amano-gawa</i></a>, <a href="/wiki/Izou" title="Izou">Izou</a>'s <i>Dangirigan</i>, and <a href="/wiki/Kikunojo" title="Kikunojo">Kikunojo</a>'s <i>Zansetsugama</i>, ultimately requiring <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin'emon">Kin'emon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denjiro" title="Denjiro">Denjiro</a>, Inuarashi, and <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> to focus and coordinate their <a href="/wiki/Oden_Two_Sword_Style#Nine_Red_Scabbards" title="Oden Two Sword Style"><i>Togen Totsuka</i></a> attacks together at his scar to finally inflict significant damage. However, Kaidou himself stated that the injuries were still shallow in comparison to when Oden inflicted him with a massive scar.<sup id="cite_ref-c993_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c993-123">[123]</a></sup> 
</p><p>This durability has given Kaidou the reputation of being unable to die. He was caught and tortured 18 times, and organizations as powerful as the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, and other Emperors have attempted to execute him 40 times, only to fail as Kaidou survived every single attempt because every execution weapon broke when used on him. Most notably, Kaidou jumped 10,000 meters from a <a href="/wiki/Sky_Island" title="Sky Island">Sky Island</a> onto the ground, creating a massive crater and shockwave strong enough to sink a large ship nearby, and emerged with only a small headache; it has even become a hobby for him to attempt suicide, only for it to fail.<sup id="cite_ref-Toughness_119-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toughness-119">[119]</a></sup> In fact, it is implied that during his early days, Kaidou allowed himself to be captured the majority of the time, due to being hungry, and used his captivity as a restaurant.<sup id="cite_ref-hungry_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hungry-124">[124]</a></sup> Kaidou also clashed with Big Mom continuously for one to three days and emerged without any injuries or signs of fatigue, showing incredible stamina.
</p><p>The first known time he ever suffered a significant injury was in a battle against <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>, a legendary samurai who was dual-wielding two of the twenty-one <a href="/wiki/Meito#21_Great_Grade_Blades" title="Meito">Great Grade Blades</a>, <a href="/wiki/Enma" title="Enma">Enma</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ame_no_Habakiri" title="Ame no Habakiri">Ame no Habakiri</a>, gaining a scar on his body.<sup id="cite_ref-c970_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970-37">[37]</a></sup> When he was simultaneously attacked by Luffy, Law, Kid, <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, and Killer, Kaidou also sustained damage. Even in his hybrid form, despite taking more lasting damage from the members of the Worst Generation, Kaidou continued fighting regularly, becoming more irritated than alarmed by their growing ability to damage him, showing that his endurance and pain tolerance are similarly anomalous like his durability. Kaidou was, however, visibly surprised at Law's ability to continually bypass his defenses, as well as Luffy's and Zoro's growing skill with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> and how both were able to seriously injure him. Despite the young pirate's increased strength and skill with Supreme King Haki infusion, however, Kaidou was still capable of defeating Luffy singlehandedly, though Kaidou admitted that the fight caused him to get more excited than he had been in a while.<sup id="cite_ref-c1013_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1013-51">[51]</a></sup> Afterwards, Kaidou clashed with his son, <a href="/wiki/Yamato" title="Yamato">Yamato</a>, a powerful warrior in his own right, and consistently overpowered him.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> Even after enduring countless powerful attacks that were greatly enhanced with advanced applications of Armament and/or Supreme King Haki, and being weakened in the process, Kaidou was still able to emerge victorious over Luffy in their third fight after landing a lethal blow, though not without unwanted assistance in the form of <a href="/wiki/Guernika" title="Guernika">Guernika</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup> Even the stone-melting flames created by his Kaen Daiko technique seemed to cause no damage or discomfort to his body in the slightest, showing a tremendous near-immunity to fire.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his enormous size, Kaidou is extremely fast in combat and can instantly move from one spot to another. He completely blitzed Luffy in an instant while attacking him and appearing behind him afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup> Another testament to his speed, he was fast enough to nearly once again blitz Luffy despite the latter perceiving the future using <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>, only barely avoiding a head-on attack.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208070737" class="image"><img alt="Uo Uo no Mi, Model Seiryu Beast Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Uo Uo no Mi, Model Seiryu Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191208070737"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20191208070737" class="image"><img alt="Uo Uo no Mi, Model Seiryu Beast Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191208070737" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Uo Uo no Mi, Model Seiryu Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2b/Uo_Uo_no_Mi%2C_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191208070737"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model_Seiryu_Beast_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou's dragon form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou ate the Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu, a <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to transform into a full serpentine Azure Dragon and a human-dragon hybrid at will.<sup id="cite_ref-c999p19_85-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c999p19-85">[85]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup> His full Beast Form is massive, roughly half the size of a <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Okobore_Town" title="Kuri">small town</a>, and is covered with extremely durable, blue scales, dramatically increasing the tremendous natural durability of Kaidou's body.<sup id="cite_ref-c939p14_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c939p14-135">[135]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1002p8_136-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1002p8-136">[136]</a></sup> His Human-Beast form grants him a massive increase to his speed, agility, and mobility, while further increasing his vast resilience and physical strength to even greater levels. 
</p><p>As a dragon, Kaidou is capable of creating special clouds called "Flame Clouds" and using them as footholds, allowing him to move through the air.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c921_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c921-138">[138]</a></sup> These clouds can also be used to lift other objects; they are even capable of lifting an <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">entire island</a> out of the sea.<sup id="cite_ref-c997_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c997-139">[139]</a></sup> He can also release devastating blasts of fire from his mouth, which can instantly deal significant damage to or fully obliterate large structures, such as an entire mountain and the ruined castle that stood upon it.<sup id="cite_ref-c922p13-15_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c922p13-15-140">[140]</a></sup> By breathing flames in the shape of a dragon around his body, Kaidou can coat himself in a layer of heat so intense that it can instantly melt substances that come in contact with it, which discourages physical attacks. Aside from his fire breath, Kaidou can also release other elemental attacks from his mouth; he can release bolts of lightning by roaring,<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup> or invisible, sharp wind blades by blowing.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup> By twisting his massive body, Kaidou can create tornados which can blow his enemies off the battlefield and into the air.<sup id="cite_ref-Tatsumaki_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tatsumaki-143">[143]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou has mastered his Devil Fruit powers to the level that he can access some of his draconic abilities without needing to transform, such as generating Flame Clouds to levitate <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c997_139-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c997-139">[139]</a></sup> He was even able to do so while battling against five members of the Worst Generation alongside Big Mom.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Kaidou is one of the few people in the world who can use all three forms of Haki; furthermore, he and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> are the only characters shown so far to be able to use the advanced applications of all three forms. Law stated that he could not directly move Kaidou around inside his <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Ope Ope no Mi">ROOM</a> due to Kaidou's Haki being too strong.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Supreme_King_Haki">Supreme King Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724112633" class="image"><img alt="Kosanze Ragnaraku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kosanze Ragnaraku.png" data-image-key="Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724112633"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724112633" class="image"><img alt="Kosanze Ragnaraku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724112633" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kosanze Ragnaraku.png" data-image-key="Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724112633"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kosanze_Ragnaraku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou imbues Hassaikai with Supreme King Haki.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou possesses immense mastery in the usage of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>. a rare form of Haki that only one in several million people in the world can use. as shown in his clash against a fellow Emperor and Supreme King Haki user, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, produced a lightning effect and burst that shook Onigashima and split the heavens.<sup id="cite_ref-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou_111-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou-111">[111]</a></sup> Additionally, Kaidou can release extremely potent bursts of Supreme King Haki that can damage the landscape around him and blow away opponents.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup>
</p><p>Most notably, he is among the small "handful" of users capable of using the advanced application of "infusing" Supreme King Haki into things, particularly, his <a href="/wiki/Hassaikai" title="Hassaikai">Hassaikai</a>, signified by the thin streams of black lightning radiating from it. When used in conjunction with his natural strength and Armament Haki, Kaidou can knock out powerful pirates, such as Luffy, Zoro, and Law in one or two strikes.<sup id="cite_ref-c923p16-17_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c923p16-17-146">[146]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kosanze_147-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kosanze-147">[147]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Supreme_King_148-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Supreme_King-148">[148]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou is an immensely skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>, which he is capable of imbuing into his kanabō. During the Raid on Onigashima, similarly to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a>, his Armament Haki was strong enough to damage Luffy, who hardened both of his arms.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> He is capable of utilizing the advanced application of this type of Haki, projecting his Armament Haki out from his kanabō, allowing him to strike opponents many meters in front of him with devastating power without the need to make direct contact,<sup id="cite_ref-Hakai_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hakai-150">[150]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kongokabura_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kongokabura-151">[151]</a></sup> and the attack power can be increased further if the kanabō is imbued with Supreme King Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-Supreme_King_148-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Supreme_King-148">[148]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, when Kaidou uses advanced Armament Haki, it is shown as a purple-colored flowing aura.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kaidou is an extremely skilled user of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>. He was able to sense the "voices" of the Super Rookies in the wake of his and Big Mom's combined attack, which enabled him to tell they were still alive.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup> He can also use the advanced application that allows him to briefly see into the future, which helps him dodge powerful blows, such as Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">"Red Hawk"</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_4_Techniques#Snakeman_2" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 4 Techniques">Snakeman</a> attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Hassaikai" title="Hassaikai">Hassaikai</a></i></dd></dl>
