<figure class="thumb tright " style="width: 68px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Hassaikai_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20191222093916" class="image"><img alt="Hassaikai Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="68" height="199" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hassaikai Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hassaikai_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Hassaikai_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/68?cb=20191222093916"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Hassaikai_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20191222093916" class="image"><img alt="Hassaikai Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Hassaikai_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/68?cb=20191222093916" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="68" height="199" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hassaikai Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hassaikai_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Hassaikai_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/68?cb=20191222093916"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaidou's Hassaikai.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kaidou wields a large, black, spiked <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kanab%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kanabō">kanabō</a> named Hassaikai as his signature weapon,<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> which he already possessed during his apprentice days in the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c957_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957-4">[4]</a></sup> Thanks to his massive strength and ability to imbue the club with Armament and Supreme King Haki,<sup id="cite_ref-Supreme_King_148-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Supreme_King-148">[148]</a></sup> Kaidou can perform incredibly powerful strikes by swinging it, allowing him to produce large shockwaves, severely injure foes,<sup id="cite_ref-Hakai_150-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hakai-150">[150]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kosanze_147-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kosanze-147">[147]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kongokabura_151-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kongokabura-151">[151]</a></sup> knock mighty adversaries unconscious with a single hit,<sup id="cite_ref-c970p14_70-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c970p14-70">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c923p16-17_146-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c923p16-17-146">[146]</a></sup> and send people flying off into the distance.<sup id="cite_ref-c824_52-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c824-52">[52]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Kaidou killed <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Oden</a>, he used a <a href="/wiki/Firearm#Pistols" title="Firearm">pistol</a> to shoot Oden in the head.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kaidou borrowed <a href="/wiki/King" title="King">King</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sword#Katana" title="Sword">katana</a> to behead <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Orochi" title="Kurozumi Orochi">Kurozumi Orochi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shuron_Hakke">Shuron Hakke</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Shuron_Hakke" title="Shuron Hakke">Shuron Hakke</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png/revision/latest?cb=20240924145805" class="image"><img alt="Warai Jogu Ragnaroku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Warai Jogu Ragnaroku.png" data-image-key="Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240924145805"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png/revision/latest?cb=20240924145805" class="image"><img alt="Warai Jogu Ragnaroku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240924145805" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Warai Jogu Ragnaroku.png" data-image-key="Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240924145805"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Warai_Jogu_Ragnaroku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shuron Hakke.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By consuming alcohol, Kaidou can enter a state called <b>Shuron Hakke</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>酒龍八卦</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>しゅろんはっけ</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Shuron Hakke</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Sake Dragon Eight Trigrams"; English adaptations: Drunken Dragon Bagua)</span>. In this state, his movements become more unpredictable, he switches rapidly between his <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a> forms, and his Haki becomes stronger.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a> vs. <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> (unseen)</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Name">Name</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D57&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kaidou's name was first officially romanized as "Kai<b>do</b>" in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup> It is shown to be spelled "Kai<b>dou</b>" in his wanted poster in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_957" title="Chapter 957">Chapter 957</a> of the manga, but the letter "U" was mostly obscured by sound effects and <a href="/wiki/Brannew" title="Brannew">Brannew</a>'s hand during the scene. In the anime depiction of the scene, Kaidou's wanted poster was not obscured, and his name was written as "Kaidou."<sup id="cite_ref-bounty_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bounty-14">[14]</a></sup> Kaidou's <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card</a> and the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.14" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.14">fourteenth</a> volume of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine" title="One Piece Magazine">One Piece Magazine</a> entry uses the "Kaidou" spelling,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-mag14_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mag14-18">[18]</a></sup> and in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_1049" title="Chapter 1049">Chapter 1049</a> and <a href="/wiki/Episode_1076" title="Episode 1076">Episode 1076</a> Kaidou's first wanted poster with the name "Kaidou" is clearly shown.<sup id="cite_ref-past_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-past-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Epithet">Epithet</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The "hyakujū"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百獣</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> part of Kaidou's epithet is an idiomatic noun meaning "all kinds of beasts/animals" (referring to the animal kingdom), combining the kanji for "hundred"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> and "beast"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">獣</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>; it is usually found in the Japanese title attributed to the lion, "hyakujū no ō"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百獣の王</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, meaning "king of beasts". With Kaidou's title an obvious derivation ("Kaidou" replacing "king"), it can be translated as "Kaidou of the Beasts". In the VIZ manga translation, as well as the subs and dub of the anime, Kaidou is instead called "Kaidou, the King of the Beasts" to make the connection more obvious.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>During his clash with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> at <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> in the manga, Kaidou was shown wearing his shirt. In the anime, he is not.<sup id="cite_ref-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou_111-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Big_Mom_vs._Kaidou-111">[111]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Support_Appearances">Support Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Great_Pirate_Colosseum" title="One Piece: Great Pirate Colosseum">One Piece: Great Pirate Colosseum</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FKaidou%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D64&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 174px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 174px; height: 132px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Kaidou_Silhouette.png/revision/latest?cb=20190603231134" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou Silhouette" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="91" height="110" data-image-name="Kaidou Silhouette.png" data-image-key="Kaidou_Silhouette.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b9/Kaidou_Silhouette.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/91?cb=20190603231134" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kaidou's original silhouette.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 174px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 174px; height: 132px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Kaidou%27s_Silhouette_in_Episode_570.png/revision/latest?cb=20200516220208" class="image"><img alt="Kaidou's Silhouette in Episode 570" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="144" height="110" data-image-name="Kaidou's Silhouette in Episode 570.png" data-image-key="Kaidou%27s_Silhouette_in_Episode_570.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Kaidou%27s_Silhouette_in_Episode_570.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/144?cb=20200516220208" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kaidou's silhouette in <a href="/wiki/Episode_570" title="Episode 570">Episode 570</a>.
</div></span></div>
<ul><li>As with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s, Kaidou's first-shown silhouettes prior to his debut greatly differed from his actual looks revealed much later:
<ul><li>His first silhouetted self was seen when the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a> were first explained by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> in <a href="/wiki/Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc" title="Post-Enies Lobby Arc">Water 7</a>, depicting Kaidou as having a much wider face, a pointier, beak-like nose, and a huge, evil-looking grin.<sup id="cite_ref-Four_Emperors_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Four_Emperors-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>When <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> briefly talked about the Four Emperors at the end of the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island_Arc" title="Fish-Man Island Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</a>, the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Anime)" title="One Piece (Anime)">anime</a> showed a similar silhouette of Kaidou as the earlier one, with his hair much puffier and wavier than it would turn out to be.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>His current look was first seen on the cover of <a href="/wiki/Chapter_693" title="Chapter 693">Chapter 693</a>, 102 chapters before his manga debut in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_795" title="Chapter 795">Chapter 795</a>.</li>
<li>The person who provided Kaidou's voice in <a href="/wiki/Episode_630" title="Episode 630">Episode 630</a> is uncredited.<sup id="cite_ref-c701_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c701-31">[31]</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Episode_739" title="Episode 739">anime episode of Kaidou's debut</a> first aired on May 1, which is also Kaidou's given birthday.</li>
<li>Kaidou's <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> is the highest currently revealed active bounty, the second highest among the Four Emperors past and present (below <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>'s), and the third highest known overall.
<ul><li>His bounty (like the other Emperors') also represents a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_wordplay#Numeric_substitution" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Japanese wordplay"><i>goroawase</i></a>-type numerical pun: in <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>4,61<b>1,10</b>0,000, the digits 110 as the whole number "one-hundred-ten" would be read as "hyakujū"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百十</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, making it homophonous with the "Beasts"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">百獣</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hyakujū</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> part of Kaidou's epithet.</li></ul></li>
<li>Kaidou seems to be inspired by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/oni" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:oni">oni</a>, ogre-like <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/y%C5%8Dkai" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:yōkai">yōkai</a> who are among the greatest icons of Japanese mythology:
<ul><li>Oni are usually depicted as having a giant, hulking frame, one or multiple horns on their heads, wild hair, and a fierce visage, traits shared by Kaidou.</li>
<li>Like Kaidou, oni are said to possess immense body strength. In addition, they are often depicted carrying <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kanab%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kanabō">kanabō</a> as their signature weapon, like Kaidou does.</li>
<li>Kaidou's residence on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> (literally "island of oni") is based on the Japanese folktale hero <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Momotar%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Momotarō">Momotarō</a>'s tale, wherein Momotarō, upon maturing into adolescence, went to defeat a band of oni dwelling on an island of said name.</li></ul></li>
<li>A resemblance of Kaidou's character can be also observed to a particular oni of Japanese myth, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shuten-d%C5%8Dji" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shuten-dōji">Shuten-dōji</a>, whose story is one of Japan's most popular oni tales (and whom <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a> is also based on):
<ul><li>Shuten-dōji was a giant, powerful oni and leader of a bandit gang who lived at Mt. Ōe in his fortress. He was born human, but as a child was referred to as a "monster child"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">怪童</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">kaidō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> for his supernatural strength and wit (which Kaidou's name may derive from, with the word "kaidō" is also translatable as "an unusually large or strong youth").</li>
<li>Since his youth, Shuten-dōji had a matchless thirst for sake (hence his name that means "sake-drinking boy") and after becoming an oni would often go on drunken rages, similar to Kaidou's own drunk persona. In fact, Kaidou's sake gourd has the kanji for "heaven"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">天</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> on it, which is also contained in a variant of the name "Shuten-dōji"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">酒天童子</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Kaidou's name may further derive from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kintar%C5%8D" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kintarō">Kintarō</a>, also called Sakata no Kintoki, another folk hero of Japanese myth. Not only is Kintarō connected to the figure of Shuten-dōji (capturing him at one point), one of his other (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edo_period" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edo period">Edo period</a>) names is "Sakata Kaidōmaru"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">坂田怪童丸</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.</li>
<li>Kaidou's rank as head of the Beasts Pirates is called "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/governor-general" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:governor-general">governor-general</a>"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">総督</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">sōtoku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, which is also translatable as simply "governor" or "viceroy". In a Japanese context, such term can refer to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ja:%E7%B7%8F%E7%9D%A3" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ja:総督">certain military commanders</a> that were active in Japan from the Bakumatsu to the early Meiji era. Additionally, from 1910 to 1945, Japanese-administered Korea had a governor-general, as did Japanese-administered Taiwan between 1895 and 1945.</li>
<li>Kaidou's belt, a twist of white rope with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shide_(Shinto)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shide (Shinto)">zigzag paper streamers</a>, is based on the ropes<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">綱</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">tsuna</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> traditionally worn by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Makuuchi#Yokozuna" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Makuuchi">yokozuna</a> (the highest-ranked sumo wrestlers, hence their name) during their entrance ceremonies so as to denote their rank. Said belts are a variation of the much larger <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/shimenawa" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:shimenawa">shimenawa</a> used to mark off sacred <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shinto" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shinto">Shinto</a> spaces like shrines; similar to the shimenawa, the yokozuna belts hold religious meaning as objects of purification.</li>
<li>Kaidou's Wano-bound reputation as a "Wise King"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">明王</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Myōō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span><sup id="cite_ref-wise_king_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wise_king-12">[12]</a></sup> is based on a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wisdom_King" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wisdom King">type of Vajrayana Buddhist deity</a>. The most popular of them in Japan is blue-skinned <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Acala#Japan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Acala">Fudō Myōō</a> who can turn into a dragon.</li>
<li>Kaidou is currently the only one of the Four Emperors whose flagship has not been seen or named.</li>
<li>Kaidou is the only Emperor who has never been seen sporting any sort of headwear.</li>
<li>Kaidou shares his Japanese voice actor with <a href="/wiki/Bear_King" title="Bear King">Bear King</a>, whose crew also had a playing card motif.</li>
<li>In the 6th and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Kaidou was ranked 97th and 65th, respectively.</li>
<li>Kaidou's favorite food is alcoholic beverages, and his least favorite is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tofu" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tofu">tofu</a>. As another favorite food,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_8-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-8">[8]</a></sup> his favorite part when eating fish is the skin.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup></li>
<li>Kaidou's hobby is attempting suicide.<sup id="cite_ref-hobby_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hobby-50">[50]</a></sup></li></ul>
